Client sends the=20

follows<BR>Security-Client:=20
ipsec-3gpp;alg=3Dhmac-md5-96;prot=3Desp;ealg=3Ddes-ede3-cbc;spi-c=3D3030;=

class=3D478533013-23022010>OpenIMS challenges=20
the UAC by sending the 401 with  Security-Server header as=20
follows<BR>Security-Server: ipsec-3gpp; ealg=3Ddes-ede3-cbc; =
alg=3Dhmac-md5-96;=20
spi-c=3D5018; spi-s=3D5019; port-c=3D4062; port-s=3D4063; prot=3Desp; =
mod=3Dtrans;=20
q=3D0.1</SPAN></FONT></DIV>
<DIV> </DIV>
<DIV><FONT face=3DArial size=3D2><SPAN class=3D478533013-23022010>UAC =
sends=20
Re_register message to the OpenIms Server from 7071 to 4063 over UDP, =
with=20
Security-Verify header as<BR>Security-Verify:=20
ipsec-3gpp;q=3D0.1;alg=3Dhmac-md5-96;prot=3Desp;ealg=3Ddes-ede3-cbc;spi-c=
=3D5018;spi-s=3D5019;port-c=3D4062;port-s=3D4063</SPAN></FONT></DIV>

sending the=20
